await tx.wait(); console.log([CrossRealm] ${signedScores.length} scores submitted for tournament ${tournamentId}); return tx; } } // ── GUN.JS SIGNATURE EXCHANGE ───────────────────────────────────────────────── /** * Players exchange signatures via Gun.js — no server needed. * * RACE RESULT COLLECTION FLOW: * * Each participant calls signRaceResult() locally. * They broadcast their sig to the Gun.js race room: * gun.get('crossrealm_races').get(raceId).get('sigs').get(myAddress).put(mySig) * * All clients listen: * gun.get('crossrealm_races').get(raceId).get('sigs').map().on((sig, addr) => { * sigMap[addr] = sig; * if (Object.keys(sigMap).length === participantCount) { * // All sigs collected — submit * signing.submitRaceResult(raceId, positions, finishedAt, orderedSigs); * } * }); * * DUEL CONCESSION FLOW: * * Loser calls signDuelConcession() — broadcasts via Gun.js to winner's client. * Winner receives it, calls submitDuelResult() immediately. * Total time from race end to REALM payout: ~15 seconds. * * DISPUTE FLOW (when loser refuses to sign): * * After DISPUTE_WINDOW (30 min), winner calls raiseRaceDuelDispute(). * Guardians review and vote. 2-of-3 resolves within 24 hours. */ // ── EXPORT ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── // Browser: window.CrossRealmSigning = CrossRealmSigning; // Module: export default CrossRealmSigning; if (typeof window !== 'undefined') { window.CrossRealmSigning = CrossRealmSigning; } CrossRealm Trustless Settlement — Dual-Sign Architecture The Problem Solved Before (V1/V2 oracle model): Race ends in Three.js → CrossRealm oracle key calls submitRaceResult() → Contract trusts the oracle → Players must trust CrossRealm runs the oracle honestly → Oracle key compromise = all race results can be faked After (V3 dual-sign model): Race ends in Three.js → Winner signs their result (their own private key) → Loser signs a concession (their own private key) → Anyone submits both sigs on-chain → Contract verifies via ecrecover — no trust required → Neither player can fake the other's signature → CrossRealm relay is optional convenience, not a trust anchor What Each Player Signs Circuit Race (multi-player) Every participant signs the same result hash: resultHash = keccak256(abi.encodePacked( "CrossRealm Race Result", // domain separator chainId, // prevents cross-chain replay contractAddress, // prevents cross-contract replay raceId, positions[], // ordered finish positions finishedAt // agreed timestamp )) All N signatures submitted in one submitSignedResult() call. Street Race Duel (1v1) Winner declares themselves. Loser signs a concession: concedeHash = keccak256(abi.encodePacked( "CrossRealm Race Concede", chainId, contractAddress, duelId, winner // who the loser is conceding to )) Winner submits submitDuelResult(duelId, winner, loserSig) . Tournament Match (bracket) Winner signs a win claim. Loser signs a concession: winHash = keccak256("CrossRealm Match Win", ..., winner, loser, finishedAt) concedeHash = keccak256("CrossRealm Match Concede", ..., winner) Either player submits submitSignedMatchResult(...) . Score Attack (shooting ranges) Each player signs their own score — nobody can sign for them: scoreHash = keccak256("CrossRealm Score", ..., player, score, timestamp) A relay or any participant submits all scores in one submitSignedScores() call. Dispute Flow If the loser refuses to sign (claims they actually won): 1. Winner calls raiseRaceDuelDispute(duelId) or raiseMatchDispute(id, matchIndex) 2. State → DISPUTED. No payout yet. 3. 2-of-3 guardian multisig reviews: - Both clients submit their replay hash to the guardians via Gun.js - Guardians watch the Three.js race replay (deterministic from Gun.js position log) - Guardians call guardianResolveDuel() or guardianVoteMatch() 4. First guardian vote sets proposed winner 5. Second guardian vote (2-of-3) triggers settlement 6. REALM paid out to correct winner Guardians can: Vote on who won a disputed match Unlock stuck races/duels (if both players disappeared) Guardians cannot: Create fake game sessions Move REALM outside the escrowed prize pool Override a result that both players already signed Affect staking, marketplace, or any other contract The Optional Relay trustedRelays is a whitelist of addresses that can submit signed results on behalf of players. This is a convenience — the CrossRealm world engine can automatically package and submit results so players don’t need to manually call the contract. The relay cannot forge signatures. It can only deliver them. If the relay is offline or compromised, either player can submit the result themselves directly. Setting up a relay: RaceContractV3.setTrustedRelay(relayAddress, true); Client Integration (Three.js world) // Initialise const signing = new CrossRealmSigning(window.provider); // When a 1v1 duel ends and local player lost: const mySig = await signing.signDuelConcession(duelId, winnerAddress); // Broadcast mySig to winner via Gun.js gun.get('crossrealm_duels').get(duelId).get('concession').put(mySig); Deployment Same constructor as V2, but now requires 3 guardian addresses: Security Properties Property Guarantee Cannot fake a win ecrecover verifies actual signer — impossible to spoof without private key Cannot replay a result resultHash includes chainId + contractAddress + raceId Cannot submit wrong positions Positions are part of the hash — changing them breaks all sigs Relay cannot cheat Relay only delivers signatures — cannot create valid ones // When winner receives loser's sig: gun.get('crossrealm_duels').get(duelId).get('concession').on(async (loserSig) => { await signing.submitDuelResult(duelId, myAddress, loserSig); // REALM in wallet within ~3 seconds }); // Score Attack — player finishes shooting range: const signedScore = await signing.signScore(tournamentId, finalScore, Date.now()); gun.get('crossrealm_scores').get(tournamentId).get(myAddress).put(JSON.stringify(signedScore)); # Deploy RaceContractV3.deploy(realm, staking, treasury, guardian0, guardian1, guardian2) TournamentBracketV2.deploy(realm, staking, treasury, guardian0, guardian1, guardian2) # Optional relay setup (for the world engine) RaceContractV3.setTrustedRelay(worldEngineAddress, true) TournamentBracketV2.setTrustedRelay(worldEngineAddress, true) # Wire trophies TrophyNFT.setAuthorisedMinter(RaceContractV3, true) TrophyNFT.setAuthorisedMinter(TournamentBracketV2, true) RaceContractV3.setTrophyNft(TrophyNFT) TournamentBracketV2.setTrophyNft(TrophyNFT) Loser cannot block payout Dispute flow resolves within 24h via guardian vote Guardian cannot steal Guards can only vote on result — prize pool is fixed at stake time Works without CrossRealm Any player can submit results directly if relay is down // SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT pragma solidity ^0.8.20; /** * ███████╗ ██████╗ ██████╗ ███████╗███████╗██████╗ █████╗ ██╗ ███╗ ███╗ * ██╔════╝██╔════╝██╔═══██╗ ██╔════╝██╔════╝██╔══██╗██╔══██╗██║ ████╗ ████║ * ██║ ██║ ██║ ██║ ███████╗███████╗██████╔╝███████║██║ ██╔████╔██║ * ██║ ██║ ██║ ██║ ╚════██║╚════██║██╔══██╗██╔══██║██║ ██║╚██╔╝██║ * ╚██████╗╚██████╗╚██████╔╝ ███████║███████║██║ ██║██║ ██║███████╗██║ ╚═╝ ██║ * ╚═════╝ ╚═════╝ ╚═════╝ ╚══════╝╚══════╝╚═╝ ╚═╝╚═╝ ╚═╝╚══════╝╚═╝ ╚═╝ * * @title AgentWallet — CrossRealm AI Twin Transaction Authority * @author CrossRealm Protocol * @notice Smart-contract wallet that gives a twin's hot-key bounded * authority to transact on behalf of the owner — fully non-custodial. * * All twin data (personality, memory, decisions) is stored LOCALLY * on the user's device via Gun.js + IndexedDB. This contract only * governs FINANCIAL AUTHORITY — what the twin is allowed to spend * and which contracts it may call. * * ─── ROLES ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── * GUARDIAN — owner's main EOA. Full control. No limits. Can kill instantly. * AGENT KEY — twin's hot-key (secure enclave / KMS). Bounded by all limits. * RECOVERY — cold backup. 48h timelock key rotation only. Cannot spend. * * ─── THREE OPERATING MODES ──────────────────────────────────────────────── * HUMAN — agent key completely disabled. Only guardian executes. * SUPERVISED — agent queues actions; guardian must approve each one on-chain. * AUTONOMOUS — agent executes immediately within limits. * * ─── SPEND HIERARCHY ────────────────────────────────────────────────────── * Every execution is checked against BOTH: * 1. Protocol hard caps (set by TwinGovernance — DAO voted) * 2. User soft limits (set by guardian — must be ≤ protocol caps) * This means users choose their comfort level within a safe protocol ceiling. * * ─── NON-CUSTODIAL GUARANTEE ────────────────────────────────────────────── * No CrossRealm server ever holds funds. * All REALM in this wallet is owned by the guardian. * Guardian can withdraw 100% at any time unconditionally. */ import "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/IERC20.sol"; import "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/utils/SafeERC20.sol"; import "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC721/IERC721.sol"; import "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC721/utils/ERC721Holder.sol"; import "@openzeppelin/contracts/security/ReentrancyGuard.sol"; // ─── INTERFACES ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── interface ITwinGovernance { struct ProtocolCaps { uint256 maxPerTx; uint256 maxDaily; uint256 minSessionTimeout; uint256 maxSessionTimeout; } function protocolCaps() external view returns (ProtocolCaps memory); function isTradingEnabled() external view returns (bool); function circuitBreakerActive() external view returns (bool); } interface ITwinRegistry { function recordAction( address agentWallet, bytes4 selector, address target, uint256 realmAmount, bytes32 actionHash ) external; function isActive(address agentWallet) external view returns (bool); } // ─── CONTRACT ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── contract AgentWallet is ReentrancyGuard, ERC721Holder { using SafeERC20 for IERC20; // ─── CONSTANTS ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────── uint256 public constant ACTION_COOLDOWN = 3 seconds; uint256 public constant RECOVERY_DELAY = 48 hours; uint256 public constant MAX_BATCH_CALLS = 5; uint256 public constant ACTION_LOG_SIZE = 100; uint256 public constant MAX_QUEUE_SIZE = 20; // ─── ENUMS ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── /// @notice The three operating modes of the twin enum AgentMode { HUMAN, SUPERVISED, AUTONOMOUS } // ─── STRUCTS ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── /** * @notice User-set spending limits. * Every value MUST be ≤ the corresponding protocol cap * at time of execution (checked live from TwinGovernance). */ struct UserLimits { uint256 maxPerTx; // max REALM per single call uint256 dailyLimit; // max REALM per rolling 24h uint256 sessionTimeoutSecs; // 0 = no timeout; else agent goes dormant bool canTrade; // MarketplaceV1 buy/list bool canDuel; // DuelContract challenge/accept bool canRace; // RaceContractV2 join/challenge bool canStake; // REALMStaking stake/unstake bool canJoinTournaments; // TournamentBracket register bool canPlayCreatorGames; // CreatorGameRegistry sessions bool canTransferRealm; // free REALM transfers (high risk — default false) bool canTransferNFT; // free NFT transfers (high risk — default false) bool canVoteDAO; // DAO voting (strongly recommend false) } /** * @notice Per-contract allowlist entry. * Empty selectors array = all function calls on this contract allowed. */ struct ContractPermission { bool allowed; bytes4[] selectors; uint256 maxValuePerCall; // 0 = governed only by dailyLimit } /** * @notice A queued action waiting for guardian approval (SUPERVISED mode). */ struct PendingAction { uint256 actionId; address target; bytes callData; uint256 realmAmount; uint256 queuedAt; bool executed; bool rejected; } /** * @notice Circular audit log entry. */ struct ActionLog { address target; bytes4 selector; uint256 realmAmount; uint256 timestamp; bool success; AgentMode modeAtExecution; } /** * @notice Pending recovery (timelocked key rotation by recovery key). */ struct RecoveryRequest { address newAgentKey; uint256 requestedAt; bool executed; } // ─── STATE ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── // Core roles address public guardian; address public agentKey; address public recoveryKey; // External contracts IERC20 public realmToken; ITwinGovernance public twinGovernance; ITwinRegistry public twinRegistry; // Mode + status AgentMode public mode; bool public paused; bool public killed; // Limits (user-set, bounded by protocol caps) UserLimits public limits; // Whitelisted contracts mapping(address => ContractPermission) public contractPermissions; address[] private _allowedContracts; // Spending tracker (rolling 24h) uint256 public dailySpent; uint256 public dailyWindowStart; // Session keepalive uint256 public lastKeepalive; uint256 public lastActionAt; // Nonce (replay protection) uint256 public nonce; // Supervised mode queue mapping(uint256 => PendingAction) public pendingActions; uint256 public pendingActionCount; uint256 public pendingActionHead; // oldest unexecuted // Audit log (circular) ActionLog[ACTION_LOG_SIZE] public actionLog; uint256 public actionLogHead; // Recovery RecoveryRequest public pendingRecovery; // ─── EVENTS ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── event ModeChanged(AgentMode oldMode, AgentMode newMode); event AgentExecuted(address target, bytes4 sel, uint256 realm, bool ok, uint256 nonce, AgentMode mode); event ActionQueued(uint256 actionId, address target, uint256 realmAmount); event ActionApproved(uint256 actionId); event ActionRejected(uint256 actionId); event GuardianExecuted(address target, uint256 value, bool ok); event LimitsUpdated(); event ContractPermissionSet(address target, bool allowed); event StatusChanged(bool paused, bool killed); event AgentKeyRotated(address oldKey, address newKey); event RecoveryInitiated(address newKey, uint256 executeAfter); event RecoveryExecuted(address newKey); event Keepalive(uint256 ts); event Deposited(address from, uint256 amount); event Withdrawn(address to, uint256 amount); // ─── MODIFIERS ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────── modifier onlyGuardian() { require(msg.sender == guardian, "Not guardian"); _; } modifier onlyAgent() { require(msg.sender == agentKey, "Not agent key"); require(!paused && !killed, "Wallet inactive"); require(mode != AgentMode.HUMAN, "Human mode — agent disabled"); require( address(twinRegistry) == address(0) || twinRegistry.isActive(address(this)), "Twin not active" ); require( address(twinGovernance) == address(0) || (!twinGovernance.circuitBreakerActive() && twinGovernance.isTradingEnabled()), "Protocol halted" ); require(block.timestamp >= lastActionAt + ACTION_COOLDOWN, "Cooldown"); require( limits.sessionTimeoutSecs == 0 || block.timestamp <= lastKeepalive + limits.sessionTimeoutSecs, "Session expired" ); _; lastActionAt = block.timestamp; } modifier notKilled() { require(!killed, "Permanently killed"); _; } // ─── CONSTRUCTOR ────────────────────────────────────────────────────── constructor( address _guardian, address _agentKey, address _recoveryKey, address _realmToken, address _twinGovernance, address _twinRegistry, UserLimits memory _limits ) { require(_guardian != address(0), "Zero guardian"); require(_agentKey != address(0), "Zero agent key"); require(_realmToken != address(0), "Zero REALM"); guardian = _guardian; agentKey = _agentKey; recoveryKey = _recoveryKey; realmToken = IERC20(_realmToken); twinGovernance = ITwinGovernance(_twinGovernance); twinRegistry = ITwinRegistry(_twinRegistry); _validateAndSetLimits(_limits); mode = AgentMode.HUMAN; // safe default — guardian must activate lastKeepalive = block.timestamp; dailyWindowStart = block.timestamp; } // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // MODE MANAGEMENT // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ /** * @notice Switch between HUMAN / SUPERVISED / AUTONOMOUS. * Guardian-only. Instant. No timelock. * You can always go from any mode back to HUMAN immediately. */ function setMode(AgentMode newMode) external onlyGuardian notKilled { AgentMode old = mode; mode = newMode; if (newMode != AgentMode.HUMAN) lastKeepalive = block.timestamp; emit ModeChanged(old, newMode); } // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // AUTONOMOUS EXECUTION (agent key, mode = AUTONOMOUS) // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ /** * @notice Twin executes a whitelisted call immediately. * Only available in AUTONOMOUS mode. * * @param target Whitelisted contract address * @param callData Encoded function call * @param realmAmount REALM to approve for this call (0 if not needed) * @param expectedNonce Replay protection */ function agentExecute( address target, bytes calldata callData, uint256 realmAmount, uint256 expectedNonce ) external onlyAgent nonReentrant returns (bool success, bytes memory returnData) { require(mode == AgentMode.AUTONOMOUS, "Not in autonomous mode"); require(expectedNonce == nonce, "Nonce mismatch"); require(callData.length >= 4, "No selector"); bytes4 sel = bytes4(callData[:4]); _checkContractPermission(target, sel); _checkActionPermission(sel, realmAmount); _checkAndUpdateSpending(realmAmount); _validateAgainstProtocolCaps(realmAmount); nonce++; if (realmAmount > 0) realmToken.safeApprove(target, realmAmount); (success, returnData) = target.call(callData); if (realmAmount > 0) realmToken.safeApprove(target, 0); _logAction(target, sel, realmAmount, success, AgentMode.AUTONOMOUS); _notifyRegistry(sel, target, realmAmount); emit AgentExecuted(target, sel, realmAmount, success, nonce - 1, AgentMode.AUTONOMOUS); } /** * @notice Batch execute (max 5 calls). All-or-nothing. */ function agentBatchExecute( address[] calldata targets, bytes[] calldata callDatas, uint256[] calldata realmAmounts, uint256 expectedNonce ) external onlyAgent nonReentrant returns (bool[] memory results) { require(mode == AgentMode.AUTONOMOUS, "Not in autonomous mode"); require(targets.length <= MAX_BATCH_CALLS, "Max 5 batch calls"); require(targets.length == callDatas.length && callDatas.length == realmAmounts.length, "Length mismatch"); require(expectedNonce == nonce, "Nonce mismatch"); uint256 total; for (uint256 i; i < realmAmounts.length; i++) total += realmAmounts[i]; _checkAndUpdateSpending(total); _validateAgainstProtocolCaps(total); results = new bool[](targets.length); nonce++; for (uint256 i; i < targets.length; i++) { require(callDatas[i].length >= 4, "No selector"); bytes4 sel = bytes4(callDatas[i][:4]); _checkContractPermission(targets[i], sel); _checkActionPermission(sel, realmAmounts[i]); if (realmAmounts[i] > 0) realmToken.safeApprove(targets[i], realmAmounts[i]); (results[i],) = targets[i].call(callDatas[i]); require(results[i], "Batch item failed"); if (realmAmounts[i] > 0) realmToken.safeApprove(targets[i], 0); _logAction(targets[i], sel, realmAmounts[i], results[i], AgentMode.AUTONOMOUS); } } // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // SUPERVISED MODE (agent queues → guardian approves on-chain) // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ /** * @notice Twin queues an action for guardian approval. * Available only in SUPERVISED mode. * Action data stored here temporarily — all memory/context * lives off-chain in the user's Gun.js local store. */ function agentQueueAction( address target, bytes calldata callData, uint256 realmAmount, uint256 expectedNonce ) external onlyAgent nonReentrant returns (uint256 actionId) { require(mode == AgentMode.SUPERVISED, "Not in supervised mode"); require(expectedNonce == nonce, "Nonce mismatch"); require(callData.length >= 4, "No selector"); require( pendingActionCount - pendingActionHead < MAX_QUEUE_SIZE, "Queue full" ); bytes4 sel = bytes4(callData[:4]); _checkContractPermission(target, sel); _checkActionPermission(sel, realmAmount); _validateAgainstProtocolCaps(realmAmount); nonce++; actionId = pendingActionCount++; pendingActions[actionId] = PendingAction({ actionId: actionId, target: target, callData: callData, realmAmount: realmAmount, queuedAt: block.timestamp, executed: false, rejected: false }); emit ActionQueued(actionId, target, realmAmount); } /** * @notice Guardian approves a queued action — executes it immediately. */ function approveAction(uint256 actionId) external onlyGuardian nonReentrant notKilled returns (bool success, bytes memory returnData) { PendingAction storage a = pendingActions[actionId]; require(!a.executed && !a.rejected, "Action already resolved"); require(a.queuedAt > 0, "Action does not exist"); a.executed = true; _checkAndUpdateSpending(a.realmAmount); bytes4 sel = bytes4(a.callData[:4]); if (a.realmAmount > 0) realmToken.safeApprove(a.target, a.realmAmount); (success, returnData) = a.target.call(a.callData); if (a.realmAmount > 0) realmToken.safeApprove(a.target, 0); _logAction(a.target, sel, a.realmAmount, success, AgentMode.SUPERVISED); _notifyRegistry(sel, a.target, a.realmAmount); emit ActionApproved(actionId); } /** * @notice Guardian rejects a queued action — it is discarded. * The rejection is stored off-chain by the twin as a learning signal. */ function rejectAction(uint256 actionId) external onlyGuardian { PendingAction storage a = pendingActions[actionId]; require(!a.executed && !a.rejected, "Already resolved"); a.rejected = true; emit ActionRejected(actionId); } // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // GUARDIAN DIRECT EXECUTION (all modes — no limits) // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ /** * @notice Guardian executes any call directly — bypasses all limits. * This is HUMAN mode's primary execution path. */ function guardianExecute( address target, bytes calldata callData, uint256 value ) external onlyGuardian nonReentrant returns (bool success, bytes memory returnData) { (success, returnData) = target.call{value: value}(callData); if (callData.length >= 4) { _logAction(target, bytes4(callData[:4]), value, success, AgentMode.HUMAN); } emit GuardianExecuted(target, value, success); } // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // KEEPALIVE // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ function keepalive() external onlyGuardian { lastKeepalive = block.timestamp; emit Keepalive(block.timestamp); } function agentKeepalive() external { require(msg.sender == agentKey, "Not agent"); require(!paused && !killed, "Inactive"); require(mode == AgentMode.AUTONOMOUS, "Autonomous only"); lastKeepalive = block.timestamp; emit Keepalive(block.timestamp); } // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // LIMIT & PERMISSION MANAGEMENT // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ function setLimits(UserLimits calldata newLimits) external onlyGuardian notKilled { _validateAndSetLimits(newLimits); emit LimitsUpdated(); } function setContractPermission( address target, bool allowed, bytes4[] calldata selectors, uint256 maxValuePerCall ) external onlyGuardian notKilled { contractPermissions[target] = ContractPermission({ allowed: allowed, selectors: selectors, maxValuePerCall: maxValuePerCall }); if (allowed) { bool found; for (uint256 i; i < _allowedContracts.length; i++) { if (_allowedContracts[i] == target) { found = true; break; } } if (!found) _allowedContracts.push(target); } emit ContractPermissionSet(target, allowed); } // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // PAUSE / KILL // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ function setPaused(bool _paused) external onlyGuardian notKilled { paused = _paused; emit StatusChanged(_paused, killed); } /** * @notice Permanently and irreversibly shut down the twin. * Guardian can still withdraw funds after killing. */ function kill() external onlyGuardian { killed = true; paused = true; mode = AgentMode.HUMAN; emit StatusChanged(true, true); } // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // KEY MANAGEMENT // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ function rotateAgentKey(address newKey) external onlyGuardian notKilled { require(newKey != address(0) && newKey != guardian, "Invalid"); emit AgentKeyRotated(agentKey, newKey); agentKey = newKey; } function initiateRecovery(address newAgentKey) external { require(msg.sender == recoveryKey, "Not recovery key"); require(newAgentKey != address(0), "Zero key"); pendingRecovery = RecoveryRequest({ newAgentKey: newAgentKey, requestedAt: block.timestamp, executed: false }); emit RecoveryInitiated(newAgentKey, block.timestamp + RECOVERY_DELAY); } function executeRecovery() external { require(msg.sender == recoveryKey, "Not recovery key"); RecoveryRequest storage r = pendingRecovery; require(!r.executed && r.requestedAt > 0, "No pending recovery"); require(block.timestamp >= r.requestedAt + RECOVERY_DELAY, "Timelock"); r.executed = true; emit AgentKeyRotated(agentKey, r.newAgentKey); emit RecoveryExecuted(r.newAgentKey); agentKey = r.newAgentKey; } function transferGuardianship(address newGuardian) external onlyGuardian { require(newGuardian != address(0) && newGuardian != agentKey); guardian = newGuardian; } // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // FUND MANAGEMENT // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ function depositRealm(uint256 amount) external { realmToken.safeTransferFrom(msg.sender, address(this), amount); emit Deposited(msg.sender, amount); } /** * @notice Withdraw REALM — unconditional, guardian only. * amount = 0 withdraws full balance. */ function withdrawRealm(uint256 amount, address to) external onlyGuardian nonReentrant { require(to != address(0)); uint256 bal = realmToken.balanceOf(address(this)); uint256 amt = amount == 0 ? bal : amount; require(amt <= bal, "Insufficient"); realmToken.safeTransfer(to, amt); emit Withdrawn(to, amt); } function withdrawNFT(address nft, uint256 tokenId, address to) external onlyGuardian nonReentrant { require(to != address(0)); IERC721(nft).safeTransferFrom(address(this), to, tokenId); } receive() external payable {} function withdrawNative(address payable to) external onlyGuardian { to.transfer(address(this).balance); } // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // INTERNAL HELPERS // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ function _validateAndSetLimits(UserLimits memory l) internal { // Fetch protocol caps and enforce ceiling if (address(twinGovernance) != address(0)) { ITwinGovernance.ProtocolCaps memory caps = twinGovernance.protocolCaps(); require(l.maxPerTx <= caps.maxPerTx, "Exceeds protocol maxPerTx cap"); require(l.dailyLimit <= caps.maxDaily, "Exceeds protocol daily cap"); if (l.sessionTimeoutSecs != 0) { require( l.sessionTimeoutSecs >= caps.minSessionTimeout && l.sessionTimeoutSecs <= caps.maxSessionTimeout, "Session timeout out of protocol range" ); } } require(l.maxPerTx > 0, "Zero maxPerTx"); require(l.dailyLimit >= l.maxPerTx, "Daily < perTx"); limits = l; } function _validateAgainstProtocolCaps(uint256 amount) internal view { if (address(twinGovernance) == address(0)) return; ITwinGovernance.ProtocolCaps memory caps = twinGovernance.protocolCaps(); require(amount <= caps.maxPerTx, "Exceeds protocol per-tx cap"); } function _checkContractPermission(address target, bytes4 sel) internal view { ContractPermission storage cp = contractPermissions[target]; require(cp.allowed, "Contract not whitelisted"); if (cp.selectors.length > 0) { bool found; for (uint256 i; i < cp.selectors.length; i++) { if (cp.selectors[i] == sel) { found = true; break; } } require(found, "Selector not whitelisted"); } if (cp.maxValuePerCall > 0) { // Checked externally via realmAmount param } } function _checkActionPermission(bytes4 sel, uint256 amount) internal view { require(amount <= limits.maxPerTx, "Exceeds user per-tx limit"); // Spot-check known high-risk selectors bytes4 TRANSFER_SEL = bytes4(keccak256("transfer(address,uint256)")); bytes4 NFT_XFR_SEL = bytes4(keccak256("safeTransferFrom(address,address,uint256)")); bytes4 VOTE_SEL = bytes4(keccak256("castVote(uint256,bool)")); bytes4 STAKE_SEL = bytes4(keccak256("stake(uint256)")); if (sel == TRANSFER_SEL && amount > 0) require(limits.canTransferRealm, "REALM transfer off"); if (sel == NFT_XFR_SEL) require(limits.canTransferNFT, "NFT transfer off"); if (sel == VOTE_SEL) require(limits.canVoteDAO, "DAO vote off"); if (sel == STAKE_SEL) require(limits.canStake, "Staking off"); } function _checkAndUpdateSpending(uint256 amount) internal { if (block.timestamp >= dailyWindowStart + 24 hours) { dailySpent = 0; dailyWindowStart = block.timestamp; } require(dailySpent + amount <= limits.dailyLimit, "Daily limit exceeded"); dailySpent += amount; } function _logAction( address target, bytes4 sel, uint256 amount, bool ok, AgentMode m ) internal { actionLog[actionLogHead % ACTION_LOG_SIZE] = ActionLog({ target: target, selector: sel, realmAmount: amount, timestamp: block.timestamp, success: ok, modeAtExecution: m }); actionLogHead++; } function _notifyRegistry(bytes4 sel, address target, uint256 amount) internal { if (address(twinRegistry) == address(0)) return; bytes32 h = keccak256(abi.encodePacked(target, sel, amount, block.timestamp, nonce)); try twinRegistry.recordAction(address(this), sel, target, amount, h) {} catch {} } // ─── VIEWS ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── function realmBalance() external view returns (uint256) { return realmToken.balanceOf(address(this)); } function getAllowedContracts() external view returns (address[] memory) { return _allowedContracts; } function getRemainingDailyBudget() external view returns (uint256) { if (block.timestamp >= dailyWindowStart + 24 hours) return limits.dailyLimit; return limits.dailyLimit > dailySpent ? limits.dailyLimit - dailySpent : 0; } function isSessionActive() external view returns (bool) { if (paused || killed || mode == AgentMode.HUMAN) return false; if (limits.sessionTimeoutSecs == 0) return true; return block.timestamp <= lastKeepalive + limits.sessionTimeoutSecs; } function getPendingAction(uint256 id) external view returns (PendingAction memory) { return pendingActions[id]; } function getActionLog(uint256 idx) external view returns (ActionLog memory) { require(idx < ACTION_LOG_SIZE); return actionLog[idx]; } function currentMode() external view returns (string memory) { if (mode == AgentMode.HUMAN) return "HUMAN"; if (mode == AgentMode.SUPERVISED) return "SUPERVISED"; return "AUTONOMOUS"; } } // SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT pragma solidity ^0.8.20; /** * @title TwinGovernance — CrossRealm AI Twin Protocol Rules * @notice The DAO-controlled rulebook that all AI twins must operate within. * * All twin DATA remains local (Gun.js + IndexedDB on user's device). * This contract only governs FINANCIAL BEHAVIOUR and PROTOCOL SAFETY. * * ─── PROTOCOL SPEND CAPS ───────────────────────────────────────────────── * Hard ceilings that no user can exceed regardless of their personal limits. * Users set their own limits WITHIN these caps (AgentWallet.UserLimits). * DAO can vote to raise/lower caps as ecosystem matures. * * DEFAULT CAPS (conservative at launch): * maxPerTx: 500 REALM (hard ceiling per single tx) * maxDaily: 10,000 REALM (hard ceiling per 24h window) * minSessionTimeout: 1 hour (session must expire eventually) * maxSessionTimeout: 30 days (max before guardian re-confirms) * * ─── CIRCUIT BREAKER ───────────────────────────────────────────────────── * Auto-pauses all twin trading if AI volume exceeds threshold. * Protects the platform from coordinated bot activity. * * ─── WASH TRADE DETECTION ──────────────────────────────────────────────── * Tracks NFT trades between twins. If the same NFT bounces between * two twins within WASH_WINDOW, both are slashed and suspended. * * ─── TWO-TIER GOVERNANCE ───────────────────────────────────────────────── * Slow path: DAO vote (existing DAOGovernance) → permanent rule changes * Fast path: protocol multisig → temporary emergency rules (max 7 days) */ import "@openzeppelin/contracts/access/Ownable.sol"; import "@openzeppelin/contracts/security/ReentrancyGuard.sol"; import "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/IERC20.sol"; import "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/utils/SafeERC20.sol"; interface ITwinRegistry { function isTwin(address aw) external view returns (bool); function isActive(address aw) external view returns (bool); function updateReputation(address aw, int256 delta, string calldata reason) external; function governanceSuspend(address aw) external; } contract TwinGovernance is Ownable, ReentrancyGuard { using SafeERC20 for IERC20; // ─── CONSTANTS ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────── uint256 public constant WASH_WINDOW = 24 hours; uint256 public constant CIRCUIT_BREAKER_COOLDOWN = 4 hours; uint256 public constant MAX_FAST_TRACK_DURATION = 7 days; int256 public constant WASH_TRADE_SLASH = -500; // ─── STRUCTS ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── /** * @notice Protocol-level hard caps. * Every AgentWallet checks these live on each execution. * UserLimits must be ≤ these values. */ struct ProtocolCaps { uint256 maxPerTx; // max REALM per single agent call uint256 maxDaily; // max REALM per rolling 24h per wallet uint256 minSessionTimeout; // minimum session lifetime (prevents permanent sessions) uint256 maxSessionTimeout; // maximum session lifetime (forces periodic re-auth) } /** * @notice Platform-wide rules for all AI twins. */ struct TwinRules { // Participation bool twinsCanDuel; bool twinsCanRace; bool twinsCanJoinTournaments; bool twinsCanListNFTs; bool twinsCanBuyNFTs; bool twinsCanPlayCreatorGames; bool twinsCanVoteDAO; // strongly recommend always false // Disclosure bool forcedDisclosureInDuels; bool forcedDisclosureInTrade; // Reputation requirements uint256 minRepForDuels; uint256 minRepForTrade; uint256 minRepForTournaments; // Volume uint16 maxAiVolumePercent; // bps — max % of platform volume from AI // Fee uint16 aiSurchargeBps; // extra fee on AI trades → staking pool bool surchargeOnDuels; bool surchargeOnRaces; // Flash uint8 maxActionsPerBlock; // per twin per block (anti-spam) } struct VolumeWindow { uint256 aiVolume; uint256 totalVolume; uint256 windowStart; } struct TradeRecord { address buyer; address seller; uint256 timestamp; } struct FastTrackRule { uint256 id; string description; uint256 activatedAt; uint256 expiresAt; bool active; } // ─── STATE ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── ProtocolCaps public protocolCaps; TwinRules public rules; ITwinRegistry public twinRegistry; IERC20 public realmToken; address public stakingPool; // Circuit breaker bool public circuitBreakerActive; uint256 public circuitBreakerAt; VolumeWindow public volumeWindow; // Surcharge accumulator (flushed to staking pool) uint256 public pendingSurcharge; // Wash trade: hash(nftContract, tokenId) → recent trades mapping(bytes32 => TradeRecord[]) private _nftTrades; // Flash limit: agentWallet → block → count mapping(address => mapping(uint256 => uint256)) public blockActions; // Fast-track emergency rules FastTrackRule[] public fastTrackRules; // Trusted reporters (marketplace, game contracts) mapping(address => bool) public trustedReporters; // Exempt twins (protocol-operated accounts, research) mapping(address => bool) public exemptTwins; // ─── EVENTS ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── event CapsUpdated(uint256 maxPerTx, uint256 maxDaily); event RulesUpdated(); event CircuitBreakerTripped(uint256 aiVol, uint256 totalVol); event CircuitBreakerLifted(); event WashTradeDetected(address twin1, address twin2, address nft, uint256 tokenId); event SurchargeCollected(address twin, uint256 amount); event SurchargeFlushed(uint256 amount); event FastTrackActivated(uint256 id, string desc, uint256 expires); event FastTrackExpired(uint256 id); event TwinExempted(address twin, bool status); // ─── CONSTRUCTOR ────────────────────────────────────────────────────── constructor( address _twinRegistry, address _realmToken, address _stakingPool ) { require(_twinRegistry != address(0) && _realmToken != address(0)); twinRegistry = ITwinRegistry(_twinRegistry); realmToken = IERC20(_realmToken); stakingPool = _stakingPool; // Conservative protocol caps at launch protocolCaps = ProtocolCaps({ maxPerTx: 500 ether, // 500 REALM hard ceiling per tx maxDaily: 10_000 ether, // 10,000 REALM hard ceiling per day minSessionTimeout: 1 hours, maxSessionTimeout: 30 days }); // Default rules — conservative at launch, loosened by DAO over time rules = TwinRules({ twinsCanDuel: true, twinsCanRace: true, twinsCanJoinTournaments: true, twinsCanListNFTs: true, twinsCanBuyNFTs: true, twinsCanPlayCreatorGames: true, twinsCanVoteDAO: false, // AI cannot vote in DAO — ever (default) forcedDisclosureInDuels: true, forcedDisclosureInTrade: false, minRepForDuels: 300, minRepForTrade: 200, minRepForTournaments: 400, maxAiVolumePercent: 3000, // 30% of platform volume aiSurchargeBps: 50, // 0.5% extra fee → stakers surchargeOnDuels: true, surchargeOnRaces: true, maxActionsPerBlock: 3 }); volumeWindow.windowStart = block.timestamp; } // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // COMPLIANCE CHECKS (called by AgentWallet + game contracts) // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ /** * @notice Check if trading is enabled globally (circuit breaker + rules). */ function isTradingEnabled() external view returns (bool) { return !circuitBreakerActive; } /** * @notice Full compliance check for a twin action. * @param agentWallet The AgentWallet requesting action * @param actionType "DUEL", "RACE", "TOURNAMENT", "BUY", "LIST", "GAME", "DAO_VOTE" * @return allowed * @return reason Human-readable reason if denied */ function checkTwinAction(address agentWallet, string calldata actionType) external view returns (bool allowed, string memory reason) { if (circuitBreakerActive) return (false, "Circuit breaker active"); if (exemptTwins[agentWallet]) return (true, ""); if (!twinRegistry.isActive(agentWallet)) return (false, "Twin not active"); bytes32 h = keccak256(bytes(actionType)); if (h == keccak256("DUEL")) { if (!rules.twinsCanDuel) return (false, "Duels disabled for twins"); } else if (h == keccak256("RACE")) { if (!rules.twinsCanRace) return (false, "Races disabled for twins"); } else if (h == keccak256("TOURNAMENT")) { if (!rules.twinsCanJoinTournaments) return (false, "Tournaments disabled"); } else if (h == keccak256("BUY")) { if (!rules.twinsCanBuyNFTs) return (false, "NFT buying disabled"); } else if (h == keccak256("LIST")) { if (!rules.twinsCanListNFTs) return (false, "NFT listing disabled"); } else if (h == keccak256("GAME")) { if (!rules.twinsCanPlayCreatorGames) return (false, "Creator games disabled"); } else if (h == keccak256("DAO_VOTE")) { if (!rules.twinsCanVoteDAO) return (false, "DAO voting disabled for AI"); } return (true, ""); } /** * @notice Compute surcharge for an AI-initiated transaction. * @param agentWallet The transacting twin * @param amount REALM amount of the transaction * @param context "TRADE", "DUEL", "RACE" */ function computeSurcharge(address agentWallet, uint256 amount, string calldata context) external view returns (uint256) { if (exemptTwins[agentWallet]) return 0; if (!twinRegistry.isTwin(agentWallet)) return 0; bytes32 h = keccak256(bytes(context)); bool apply = (h == keccak256("TRADE")) || (h == keccak256("DUEL") && rules.surchargeOnDuels) || (h == keccak256("RACE") && rules.surchargeOnRaces); return apply ? (amount * rules.aiSurchargeBps) / 10_000 : 0; } /** * @notice Flash limit check — is this twin under its per-block action cap? */ function checkFlashLimit(address agentWallet) external view returns (bool) { return blockActions[agentWallet][block.number] < rules.maxActionsPerBlock; } // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // VOLUME REPORTING (marketplace + game contracts call this) // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ /** * @notice Report a completed transaction for circuit breaker + wash trade tracking. * * @param agentWallet AgentWallet that initiated (address(0) = human) * @param nftContract NFT traded (address(0) = not an NFT trade) * @param tokenId NFT token ID * @param realmAmount REALM volume * @param counterparty Other party in trade (address(0) if unknown) */ function reportTransaction( address agentWallet, address nftContract, uint256 tokenId, uint256 realmAmount, address counterparty ) external nonReentrant { require(trustedReporters[msg.sender], "Not trusted reporter"); bool isTwinTx = agentWallet != address(0) && twinRegistry.isTwin(agentWallet); // Rolling 1-hour volume window if (block.timestamp >= volumeWindow.windowStart + 1 hours) { volumeWindow.aiVolume = 0; volumeWindow.totalVolume = 0; volumeWindow.windowStart = block.timestamp; } volumeWindow.totalVolume += realmAmount; if (isTwinTx) { volumeWindow.aiVolume += realmAmount; blockActions[agentWallet][block.number]++; } // Circuit breaker if (!circuitBreakerActive && volumeWindow.totalVolume > 0) { uint256 pct = (volumeWindow.aiVolume * 10_000) / volumeWindow.totalVolume; if (pct > rules.maxAiVolumePercent) { circuitBreakerActive = true; circuitBreakerAt = block.timestamp; emit CircuitBreakerTripped(volumeWindow.aiVolume, volumeWindow.totalVolume); } } // Wash trade check if (isTwinTx && nftContract != address(0) && counterparty != address(0)) { _checkWashTrade(agentWallet, counterparty, nftContract, tokenId); } // Surcharge accumulation if (isTwinTx && !exemptTwins[agentWallet]) { uint256 sc = (realmAmount * rules.aiSurchargeBps) / 10_000; if (sc > 0) { pendingSurcharge += sc; emit SurchargeCollected(agentWallet, sc); } } } function _checkWashTrade( address twin1, address counterparty, address nftContract, uint256 tokenId ) internal { if (!twinRegistry.isTwin(counterparty)) return; bytes32 key = keccak256(abi.encodePacked(nftContract, tokenId)); TradeRecord[] storage history = _nftTrades[key]; for (uint256 i; i < history.length; i++) { if (block.timestamp > history[i].timestamp + WASH_WINDOW) continue; if ((history[i].buyer == twin1 && history[i].seller == counterparty) || (history[i].buyer == counterparty && history[i].seller == twin1)) { // WASH TRADE twinRegistry.updateReputation(twin1, WASH_TRADE_SLASH, "Wash trade"); twinRegistry.updateReputation(counterparty, WASH_TRADE_SLASH, "Wash trade"); emit WashTradeDetected(twin1, counterparty, nftContract, tokenId); return; } } // Record trade (keep last 10) if (history.length >= 10) { for (uint256 i; i < 9; i++) history[i] = history[i + 1]; history[history.length - 1] = TradeRecord(twin1, counterparty, block.timestamp); } else { history.push(TradeRecord(twin1, counterparty, block.timestamp)); } } // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // CIRCUIT BREAKER // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ function liftCircuitBreaker() external { require(circuitBreakerActive, "Not active"); require( block.timestamp >= circuitBreakerAt + CIRCUIT_BREAKER_COOLDOWN || owner() == msg.sender, "Cooldown not passed" ); circuitBreakerActive = false; volumeWindow.aiVolume = 0; volumeWindow.totalVolume = 0; volumeWindow.windowStart = block.timestamp; emit CircuitBreakerLifted(); } // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // FAST-TRACK EMERGENCY RULES // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ function activateFastTrack(string calldata desc, uint256 durationSecs) external onlyOwner returns (uint256 id) { require(durationSecs > 0 && durationSecs <= MAX_FAST_TRACK_DURATION); id = fastTrackRules.length; fastTrackRules.push(FastTrackRule({ id: id, description: desc, activatedAt: block.timestamp, expiresAt: block.timestamp + durationSecs, active: true })); emit FastTrackActivated(id, desc, block.timestamp + durationSecs); } function expireFastTrack(uint256 id) external { FastTrackRule storage r = fastTrackRules[id]; require(r.active, "Not active"); require(block.timestamp >= r.expiresAt || owner() == msg.sender); r.active = false; emit FastTrackExpired(id); } // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // SURCHARGE FLUSH // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ function flushSurcharge() external nonReentrant { uint256 amt = pendingSurcharge; require(amt > 0, "Nothing"); pendingSurcharge = 0; realmToken.safeTransfer(stakingPool, amt); emit SurchargeFlushed(amt); } // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // RULE MANAGEMENT (owner = DAO governance contract / multisig) // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ /** * @notice DAO updates the protocol hard caps. * Any AgentWallet with limits above new caps will fail at next execution. */ function setProtocolCaps( uint256 maxPerTx, uint256 maxDaily, uint256 minSession, uint256 maxSession ) external onlyOwner { require(maxPerTx > 0 && maxDaily >= maxPerTx, "Invalid caps"); require(minSession <= maxSession, "Session range invalid"); protocolCaps = ProtocolCaps(maxPerTx, maxDaily, minSession, maxSession); emit CapsUpdated(maxPerTx, maxDaily); } function setTwinRules(TwinRules calldata newRules) external onlyOwner { require(newRules.maxAiVolumePercent <= 10_000, "Bad volume pct"); require(newRules.aiSurchargeBps <= 500, "Surcharge max 5%"); require(newRules.maxActionsPerBlock >= 1 && newRules.maxActionsPerBlock <= 10, "Bad block limit"); rules = newRules; emit RulesUpdated(); } // Granular setters for DAO proposals function setCanVoteDAO(bool val) external onlyOwner { rules.twinsCanVoteDAO = val; } function setCanDuel(bool val) external onlyOwner { rules.twinsCanDuel = val; } function setCanRace(bool val) external onlyOwner { rules.twinsCanRace = val; } function setAiSurchargeBps(uint16 bps) external onlyOwner { require(bps <= 500); rules.aiSurchargeBps = bps; } function setMaxAiVolumePercent(uint16 bps) external onlyOwner { require(bps <= 10_000); rules.maxAiVolumePercent = bps; } function setMinRep(uint256 duels, uint256 trade, uint256 tournaments) external onlyOwner { rules.minRepForDuels = duels; rules.minRepForTrade = trade; rules.minRepForTournaments = tournaments; } function setExemptTwin(address twin, bool exempt) external onlyOwner { exemptTwins[twin] = exempt; emit TwinExempted(twin, exempt); } function setTrustedReporter(address r, bool t) external onlyOwner { trustedReporters[r] = t; } function setStakingPool(address sp) external onlyOwner { require(sp != address(0)); stakingPool = sp; } // ─── VIEWS ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── function getProtocolCaps() external view returns (ProtocolCaps memory) { return protocolCaps; } function getTwinRules() external view returns (TwinRules memory) { return rules; } function getVolumeWindow() external view returns (VolumeWindow memory) { return volumeWindow; } function getAiVolumePct() external view returns (uint256) { if (volumeWindow.totalVolume == 0) return 0; return (volumeWindow.aiVolume * 10_000) / volumeWindow.totalVolume; } function getFastTrackCount() external view returns (uint256) { return fastTrackRules.length; } } // SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT pragma solidity ^0.8.20; /** * @title AgentWalletFactory — CrossRealm Twin Deployment * @notice One-call deployment of a fully wired AgentWallet + TwinRegistry entry. * * Handles: * 1. AgentWallet deployment with user limits (validated against protocol caps) * 2. Pre-whitelist all CrossRealm protocol contracts * 3. TwinRegistry registration with LLM provider + data anchors * 4. Initial REALM budget deposit * * Deploy fee (REALM) → staking pool. * Every new twin makes existing stakers richer. * * NON-CUSTODIAL: Factory never holds user funds. * The AgentWallet is owned by the caller from the moment of deployment. */ import "./AgentWallet.sol"; import "@openzeppelin/contracts/access/Ownable.sol"; import "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/IERC20.sol"; import "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/utils/SafeERC20.sol"; interface ITwinRegistryDeploy { enum LLMProvider { CLAUDE, GPT4, GEMINI, LLAMA_LOCAL, MISTRAL, GROK, CUSTOM } function registerTwin( address agentWallet, string calldata name, uint8 llmProvider, string calldata llmProviderName, bytes32 personalityHash, string calldata memoryAnchor, string calldata avatarUri, bool disclosureReq, bool localModelOnly, address beneficiary, uint256 inactivityTimeout ) external returns (bool); } contract AgentWalletFactory is Ownable { using SafeERC20 for IERC20; // ─── STATE ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── IERC20 public realmToken; address public twinRegistry; address public twinGovernance; address public stakingPool; uint256 public deployFee; // REALM — anti-spam, goes to staking pool // CrossRealm protocol contracts — pre-whitelisted on every new wallet address[] public protocolContracts; // Registry mapping(address => address[]) public ownerWallets; // owner → deployed wallets address[] public allWallets; // ─── EVENTS ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── event TwinDeployed( address indexed owner, address indexed agentWallet, address indexed agentKey, string name, uint8 llmProvider ); event ProtocolContractAdded(address contractAddr); event ProtocolContractRemoved(address contractAddr); event DeployFeeUpdated(uint256 fee); // ─── CONSTRUCTOR ────────────────────────────────────────────────────── constructor( address _realm, address _twinRegistry, address _twinGovernance, address _stakingPool, uint256 _deployFee ) { require(_realm != address(0) && _twinRegistry != address(0)); realmToken = IERC20(_realm); twinRegistry = _twinRegistry; twinGovernance = _twinGovernance; stakingPool = _stakingPool; deployFee = _deployFee; } // ─── DEPLOYMENT ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────── /** * @notice Deploy an AgentWallet and register a twin — one transaction. * * @param agentKey Twin's hot signing key (generated off-chain in secure enclave) * @param recoveryKey Cold backup key for key rotation (can be address(0)) * @param limits User spending limits (must be ≤ protocol caps) * @param twinName Display name (max 32 chars) * @param llmProvider Which AI powers this twin (0=Claude,1=GPT4,2=Gemini, * 3=LlamaLocal,4=Mistral,5=Grok,6=Custom) * @param llmProviderName Custom provider name string (only if llmProvider == 6) * @param personalityHash keccak256(personality.json) — proves training data * Pass bytes32(0) if personality not yet built * @param memoryAnchor IPFS CID of initial memory snapshot (can be "") * @param avatarUri IPFS GLB avatar (can be "") * @param disclosureReq Twin must identify as AI in world interactions * @param localModelOnly True if using local Llama/Ollama (no external API) * @param initialBudget REALM to deposit as spending budget (can be 0) * @param beneficiary Dead man's switch recipient (address(0) = disabled) * @param inactivityTimeout Seconds before dead man's switch activates (0 = disabled) */ function deployTwin( address agentKey, address recoveryKey, AgentWallet.UserLimits calldata limits, string calldata twinName, uint8 llmProvider, string calldata llmProviderName, bytes32 personalityHash, string calldata memoryAnchor, string calldata avatarUri, bool disclosureReq, bool localModelOnly, uint256 initialBudget, address beneficiary, uint256 inactivityTimeout ) external returns (address agentWalletAddr) { require(agentKey != address(0) && agentKey != msg.sender, "Bad agent key"); require(llmProvider <= 6, "Unknown LLM provider"); // Collect deploy fee → staking pool (anti-spam + staker reward) if (deployFee > 0) { realmToken.safeTransferFrom(msg.sender, stakingPool, deployFee); } // Deploy AgentWallet AgentWallet wallet = new AgentWallet( msg.sender, // guardian = caller agentKey, recoveryKey, address(realmToken), twinGovernance, twinRegistry, limits ); agentWalletAddr = address(wallet); // Pre-whitelist all CrossRealm protocol contracts for (uint256 i; i < protocolContracts.length; i++) { wallet.setContractPermission( protocolContracts[i], true, new bytes4[](0), // all selectors 0 // no per-call cap (daily limit governs) ); } // Deposit initial REALM budget if (initialBudget > 0) { realmToken.safeTransferFrom(msg.sender, agentWalletAddr, initialBudget); } // Register in TwinRegistry ITwinRegistryDeploy(twinRegistry).registerTwin( agentWalletAddr, twinName, llmProvider, llmProviderName, personalityHash, memoryAnchor, avatarUri, disclosureReq, localModelOnly, beneficiary, inactivityTimeout ); ownerWallets[msg.sender].push(agentWalletAddr); allWallets.push(agentWalletAddr); emit TwinDeployed(msg.sender, agentWalletAddr, agentKey, twinName, llmProvider); } // ─── VIEWS ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── function getOwnerWallets(address owner) external view returns (address[] memory) { return ownerWallets[owner]; Deployall.s SOL Racecontractv3 SOL Tournamentbracketv2 SOL Duelcontract SOL Marketplacev1 SOL Trophynft SOL Assetnft SOL Storefrontmanager SOL Worldregistry SOL Physicalnft SOL Creatorregistry SOL Avatarregistry SOL Creatorgameregistry SOL Eightballverifier complete SOL Penaltyverifier complete SOL Tournament realm SOL // SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT pragma solidity ^0.8.24; /** * @title StealthKeyRegistry — CrossRealm Anonymous LP Privacy Layer * * PURPOSE: * Implements ERC-5564 stealth meta-address standard. * Users register public keys once. Senders derive one-time stealth * wallets from those keys off-chain. The registry stores announcements * so recipients can scan and identify their own stealth wallets. * * HOW IT FITS IN THE FULL PRIVACY MODEL: * * Layer 1 — StealthKeyRegistry (this contract): * Master wallet calls registerStealthKeys() once. * Browser generates ephemeral keypair + derives stealth wallet S. * Browser calls announce(stealthAddress, ephemeralPubKey) on-chain. * Master wallet scans announcements to find its stealth wallets. * * Layer 2 — PrivateLPVault_v2: * Stealth wallet S (or claimer paying gas) calls deposit(commitment). * commitment = keccak256(nullifier, secret) generated in browser. * No wallet address ever stored — only the hash. * * Layer 3 — Nullifier claim: * Any wallet presents nullifier + secret to withdraw. * CORE + REALM + game rewards released to any recipient address. * * WHAT THIS MEANS ON-CHAIN: * Analyst sees: wallet S deposited. Who is S? They cannot tell * without the master wallet's private key (needed to derive S). * Even if S is identified, the commitment scheme breaks the link * to the claiming wallet. * * DEPLOYMENT: * Simple deploy — no constructor args, no dependencies. * Owner: deployer (0x73a6). Can be set to DAO later. * * POST-TGE V2 (Option B — Groth16 ZK): * Full amount privacy via circom circuits + trusted setup ceremony. * Will be proposed as a DAO governance upgrade once volume is established. * The registry is forward-compatible — no changes needed. */ contract StealthKeyRegistry { // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // TYPES // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ struct StealthMetaAddress { bytes spendingPubKey; // 33 bytes compressed secp256k1 bytes viewingPubKey; // 33 bytes compressed secp256k1 uint256 registeredAt; bool exists; } struct Announcement { address stealthAddress; // the derived one-time wallet bytes ephemeralPubKey; // 33 bytes: R = r*G bytes metadata; // optional: encrypted amount/token hint for recipient uint256 timestamp; } // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // STATE // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // master wallet → stealth meta-address mapping(address => StealthMetaAddress) private _metaAddresses; // all announcements — recipients scan this array Announcement[] private _announcements; // stealthAddress → master (reverse lookup, set only by master) // optional: master can register their stealth address here for // faster lookup without scanning all announcements mapping(address => address) public stealthToMaster; // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // EVENTS // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ event StealthKeysRegistered( address indexed registrant, bytes spendingPubKey, bytes viewingPubKey ); event StealthKeysUpdated( address indexed registrant, bytes spendingPubKey, bytes viewingPubKey ); event StealthAddressAnnounced( address indexed stealthAddress, bytes ephemeralPubKey, uint256 announcementIndex ); // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // REGISTRATION // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ /** * @notice Register or update stealth meta-address keys. * Call once from master wallet. Can be updated any time. * * @param _spendingPubKey Compressed secp256k1 key (33 bytes) * Used to derive stealth wallet private key * @param _viewingPubKey Compressed secp256k1 key (33 bytes) * Used by sender for ECDH shared secret * * BROWSER GENERATION: * const wallet = ethers.Wallet.createRandom(); * spendingPubKey = wallet.signingKey.compressedPublicKey // 33 bytes * viewingPubKey = ethers.Wallet.createRandom().signingKey.compressedPublicKey * Store both private keys encrypted — needed to scan + claim. */ function registerStealthKeys( bytes calldata _spendingPubKey, bytes calldata _viewingPubKey ) external { require(_spendingPubKey.length == 33, "Spending key must be 33 bytes"); require(_viewingPubKey.length == 33, "Viewing key must be 33 bytes"); bool isNew = !_metaAddresses[msg.sender].exists; _metaAddresses[msg.sender] = StealthMetaAddress({ spendingPubKey: _spendingPubKey, viewingPubKey: _viewingPubKey, registeredAt: block.timestamp, exists: true }); if (isNew) { emit StealthKeysRegistered(msg.sender, _spendingPubKey, _viewingPubKey); } else { emit StealthKeysUpdated(msg.sender, _spendingPubKey, _viewingPubKey); } } // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // ANNOUNCEMENTS // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ /** * @notice Publish an announcement so the stealth wallet owner can find it. * Called by the browser after deriving the stealth address. * Anyone can announce — no auth needed. * * @param _stealthAddress The derived one-time wallet address * @param _ephemeralPubKey Ephemeral public key R = r*G (33 bytes) * r was the random scalar used to derive the stealth wallet * @param _metadata Optional: encrypted payment details for recipient * Can be empty (0x) */ function announce( address _stealthAddress, bytes calldata _ephemeralPubKey, bytes calldata _metadata ) external { require(_stealthAddress != address(0), "Zero stealth address"); require(_ephemeralPubKey.length == 33, "Ephemeral key must be 33 bytes"); uint256 idx = _announcements.length; _announcements.push(Announcement({ stealthAddress: _stealthAddress, ephemeralPubKey: _ephemeralPubKey, metadata: _metadata, timestamp: block.timestamp })); emit StealthAddressAnnounced(_stealthAddress, _ephemeralPubKey, idx); } /** * @notice Convenience: announce + register stealth→master mapping in one tx. * Only callable by the master wallet to prevent spoofing. */ function announceAndRegister( address _stealthAddress, bytes calldata _ephemeralPubKey, bytes calldata _metadata ) external { require(_stealthAddress != address(0), "Zero stealth address"); require(_ephemeralPubKey.length == 33, "Ephemeral key must be 33 bytes"); require(_metaAddresses[msg.sender].exists, "Register keys first"); stealthToMaster[_stealthAddress] = msg.sender; uint256 idx = _announcements.length; _announcements.push(Announcement({ stealthAddress: _stealthAddress, ephemeralPubKey: _ephemeralPubKey, metadata: _metadata, timestamp: block.timestamp })); emit StealthAddressAnnounced(_stealthAddress, _ephemeralPubKey, idx); } // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // VIEW FUNCTIONS // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ function getStealthMetaAddress(address _master) external view returns ( bytes memory spendingPubKey, bytes memory viewingPubKey, uint256 registeredAt, bool exists ) { StealthMetaAddress storage sma = _metaAddresses[_master]; return (sma.spendingPubKey, sma.viewingPubKey, sma.registeredAt, sma.exists); } function getAnnouncementCount() external view returns (uint256) { return _announcements.length; } function getAnnouncement(uint256 _idx) external view returns ( address stealthAddress, bytes memory ephemeralPubKey, bytes memory metadata, uint256 timestamp ) { require(_idx < _announcements.length, "Index out of range"); Announcement storage a = _announcements[_idx]; return (a.stealthAddress, a.ephemeralPubKey, a.metadata, a.timestamp); } /** * @notice Batch fetch announcements for efficient off-chain scanning. * Scanner passes its last known index to only fetch new ones. */ function getAnnouncementsRange( uint256 _from, uint256 _to ) external view returns (Announcement[] memory) { require(_to <= _announcements.length, "End out of range"); require(_from < _to, "Invalid range"); Announcement[] memory result = new Announcement[](_to - _from); for (uint256 i = _from; i < _to; i++) { result[i - _from] = _announcements[i]; } return result; } /** * @notice Check if a master wallet has registered keys. */ function isRegistered(address _master) external view returns (bool) { return _metaAddresses[_master].exists; } }. // SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT pragma solidity ^0.8.24; import "@openzeppelin/contracts/security/ReentrancyGuard.sol"; import "@openzeppelin/contracts/access/Ownable.sol"; import "@openzeppelin/contracts/security/Pausable.sol"; import "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/IERC20.sol"; /** * @title PrivateLPVault_v2 — CrossRealm Anonymous Liquidity Vault * * WHAT IT DOES: * Anonymous LPs deposit CORE. The vault pairs it with REALM from its * reserve (funded by dev from the 3.6M allocation), adds liquidity * to the REALM/CORE IceCreamSwap pool, and holds the LP tokens. * * LP providers earn two yield streams: * 1. IceCreamSwap trading fees (auto-compounded in LP token value) * 2. A share of CrossRealm game dev cut (REALM, via Masterchef accounting) * * Privacy model: wallet address never stored. Only a commitment hash. * Deposit from wallet A. Claim from wallet Z. No on-chain link. * * HOW IT WORKS: * 1. User generates: commitment = keccak256(nullifier, secret) [in browser] * 2. User calls deposit(commitment) with CORE * 3. Vault pairs CORE + REALM → IceCreamSwap → receives LP tokens * 4. LP tokens stored against commitment hash (not wallet address) * 5. Game fees route here via receiveGameRewards() * 6. Rewards accumulate per-commitment via Masterchef accRewardPerShare * 7. User calls withdraw(nullifier, secret, recipient) from ANY wallet * 8. LP tokens redeemed → CORE + REALM returned + game rewards released * * REALM RESERVE: * Dev funds via fundRealm() from the ~3.6M DEX allocation. * Not all 3.6M — dev decides how much to seed. * Can top up at any time. DAO can also call fundRealm() via proposal. * * LP POOL ADDRESS: * Set at deploy via constructor. This is the REALM/WCORЕ IceCreamSwap * pair that you create and seed first. The vault holds LP tokens * from THIS specific pool only. * * DEPLOYMENT ORDER: * 1. Create REALM/CORE pool on IceCreamSwap (seed $50 CORE, burn LP) * 2. Deploy PrivateLPVault_v2(realmToken, iceCreamRouter, lpTokenAddress) * 3. Deploy TokenGateway_v2(..., privateLPVault address) * 4. Call fundRealm(amount) to seed the REALM pairing reserve * 5. Wire Rewards_REALM to call receiveGameRewards() via setPrivateLPVault() * * DEX: * IceCreamSwap router on Core Mainnet: 0xBb5e1777A331ED93E07cF043363e1d7d924e050a */ interface IUniswapV2Router { function addLiquidityETH( address token, uint256 amountTokenDesired, uint256 amountTokenMin, uint256 amountETHMin, address to, uint256 deadline ) external payable returns (uint256 amountToken, uint256 amountETH, uint256 liquidity); function removeLiquidityETH( address token, uint256 liquidity, uint256 amountTokenMin, uint256 amountETHMin, address to, uint256 deadline ) external returns (uint256 amountToken, uint256 amountETH); function getAmountsOut( uint256 amountIn, address[] calldata path ) external view returns (uint256[] memory amounts); function WETH() external pure returns (address); } contract PrivateLPVault_v2 is ReentrancyGuard, Ownable, Pausable { // ─── CONSTANTS ─────────────────────────────────────────── uint256 public constant MERKLE_TREE_HEIGHT = 20; // up to 1M positions uint256 public constant SLIPPAGE_BPS = 300; // 3% uint256 public constant BASIS_POINTS = 10_000; bytes32 public constant DOMAIN_TYPEHASH = keccak256( "EIP712Domain(string name,string version,uint256 chainId,address verifyingContract)" ); bytes32 public constant DEPOSIT_TYPEHASH = keccak256( "DepositIntent(bytes32 commitment,uint256 coreAmount,uint256 deadline,uint256 nonce)" ); // ─── IMMUTABLES ────────────────────────────────────────── IERC20 public immutable realmToken; address public immutable router; // IceCreamSwap router address public immutable lpToken; // REALM/CORE LP token address bytes32 public immutable DOMAIN_SEPARATOR; // ─── PRIVACY STATE ─────────────────────────────────────── mapping(bytes32 => bool) public commitments; // commitment → exists mapping(bytes32 => bool) public nullifierHashes; // nullifierHash → spent mapping(bytes32 => uint256) public lpShares; // commitment → LP tokens held // Merkle tree (incremental) bytes32[MERKLE_TREE_HEIGHT] public filledSubtrees; bytes32 public root; uint256 public nextIndex; // Meta-tx nonces mapping(address => uint256) public nonces; // ─── MASTERCHEF REWARD TRACKING ────────────────────────── uint256 public accRewardPerShare; // scaled 1e12 uint256 public totalLpShares; // total LP tokens across all commitments mapping(bytes32 => uint256) public rewardDebt; mapping(bytes32 => uint256) public pendingExtra; // accumulated before debt calc // ─── REALM RESERVE (for pairing with deposits) ─────────── uint256 public realmReserve; // ─── AUTHORISED REWARD SENDERS ─────────────────────────── mapping(address => bool) public rewardSenders; // Rewards_REALM contract // ─── STATS ─────────────────────────────────────────────── uint256 public totalDeposited; uint256 public totalLpMinted; uint256 public activeCommitments; uint256 public totalGameRewardsDistributed; // ─── EVENTS ────────────────────────────────────────────── event Deposit( bytes32 indexed commitment, uint256 leafIndex, uint256 coreAmount, uint256 realmPaired, uint256 lpMinted, uint256 timestamp ); event Withdrawal( bytes32 indexed nullifierHash, address indexed recipient, uint256 coreReceived, uint256 realmFromLP, uint256 gameRewardsClaimed ); event RealmFunded(address indexed funder, uint256 amount); event GameRewardsReceived(uint256 amount, uint256 newAccPerShare); event RewardSenderSet(address indexed sender, bool status); // ─── CONSTRUCTOR ───────────────────────────────────────── constructor( address _realmToken, address _router, address _lpToken ) { require(_realmToken != address(0), "Zero realm"); require(_router != address(0), "Zero router"); require(_lpToken != address(0), "Zero lp token"); realmToken = IERC20(_realmToken); router = _router; lpToken = _lpToken; DOMAIN_SEPARATOR = keccak256(abi.encode( DOMAIN_TYPEHASH, keccak256("PrivateLPVault"), keccak256("2"), block.chainid, address(this) )); // Init Merkle tree with zero-value hashes bytes32 cur = keccak256(abi.encodePacked(uint256(0))); for (uint256 i = 0; i < MERKLE_TREE_HEIGHT; i++) { filledSubtrees[i] = cur; cur = keccak256(abi.encodePacked(cur, cur)); } root = cur; } // ─── DEPOSIT (direct) ──────────────────────────────────── /** * @notice Deposit CORE and get an anonymous LP position. * @param _commitment keccak256(nullifier, secret) — generated in browser * Save nullifier + secret encrypted. Losing = losing funds. */ function deposit(bytes32 _commitment) external payable nonReentrant whenNotPaused { _processDeposit(_commitment, msg.value); } // ─── DEPOSIT (meta-tx — claimer pays gas) ──────────────── /** * @notice Meta-transaction deposit. Stealth wallet signs, claimer submits. * Claimer pays gas AND sends msg.value == coreAmount. * Claimer will later claim rewards — economically incentivised. */ function depositWithSignature( bytes32 _commitment, uint256 _coreAmount, uint256 _deadline, address _stealthAddr, uint8 _v, bytes32 _r, bytes32 _s ) external payable nonReentrant whenNotPaused { require(block.timestamp <= _deadline, "Signature expired"); require(msg.value == _coreAmount, "Value mismatch"); bytes32 structHash = keccak256(abi.encode( DEPOSIT_TYPEHASH, _commitment, _coreAmount, _deadline, nonces[_stealthAddr] )); bytes32 digest = keccak256(abi.encodePacked( "\x19\x01", DOMAIN_SEPARATOR, structHash )); address signer = ecrecover(digest, _v, _r, _s); require(signer == _stealthAddr && signer != address(0), "Invalid signature"); nonces[_stealthAddr]++; _processDeposit(_commitment, _coreAmount); } // ─── INTERNAL DEPOSIT ──────────────────────────────────── function _processDeposit(bytes32 _commitment, uint256 _coreAmount) internal { require(_coreAmount >= 0.001 ether, "Min 0.001 CORE"); require(!commitments[_commitment], "Commitment exists"); require(nextIndex < 2**MERKLE_TREE_HEIGHT, "Tree full"); // Quote REALM needed at current pool ratio uint256 realmNeeded = _quoteRealmForCore(_coreAmount); require(realmReserve >= realmNeeded, "REALM reserve insufficient — owner must call fundRealm()"); realmReserve -= realmNeeded; realmToken.approve(router, realmNeeded); uint256 minRealm = realmNeeded * (BASIS_POINTS - SLIPPAGE_BPS) / BASIS_POINTS; uint256 minCore = _coreAmount * (BASIS_POINTS - SLIPPAGE_BPS) / BASIS_POINTS; // Add liquidity — LP tokens stay in this contract (uint256 realmUsed, , uint256 lpMinted) = IUniswapV2Router(router) .addLiquidityETH{value: _coreAmount}( address(realmToken), realmNeeded, minRealm, minCore, address(this), block.timestamp + 10 minutes ); // Refund any unused REALM back to reserve if (realmNeeded > realmUsed) { realmReserve += (realmNeeded - realmUsed); } // Record commitment — no wallet address stored uint256 leafIndex = nextIndex; _insertLeaf(_commitment); commitments[_commitment] = true; lpShares[_commitment] = lpMinted; rewardDebt[_commitment] = (lpMinted * accRewardPerShare) / 1e12; totalLpShares += lpMinted; totalDeposited += _coreAmount; totalLpMinted += lpMinted; activeCommitments++; emit Deposit(_commitment, leafIndex, _coreAmount, realmUsed, lpMinted, block.timestamp); } // ─── WITHDRAW ──────────────────────────────────────────── /** * @notice Present nullifier + secret from ANY wallet to claim funds. * Redeems LP tokens → CORE + REALM returned at current market rate. * Accumulated game rewards also released. * @param _nullifier First half of commitment preimage * @param _secret Second half of commitment preimage * @param _recipient Address to receive everything (can be any address) */ function withdraw( bytes32 _nullifier, bytes32 _secret, address payable _recipient ) external nonReentrant whenNotPaused { require(_recipient != address(0), "Zero recipient"); bytes32 commitment = keccak256(abi.encodePacked(_nullifier, _secret)); bytes32 nullifierHash = keccak256(abi.encodePacked(_nullifier)); require(commitments[commitment], "Commitment not found"); require(!nullifierHashes[nullifierHash], "Already withdrawn"); // Mark spent before any transfers nullifierHashes[nullifierHash] = true; uint256 lp = lpShares[commitment]; uint256 accrued = (lp * accRewardPerShare) / 1e12; uint256 debt = rewardDebt[commitment]; uint256 gameRew = accrued > debt ? accrued - debt + pendingExtra[commitment] : pendingExtra[commitment]; // Clean up totalLpShares -= lp; lpShares[commitment] = 0; rewardDebt[commitment] = 0; pendingExtra[commitment] = 0; activeCommitments--; // Approve router to spend LP tokens IERC20(lpToken).approve(router, lp); // Remove liquidity — CORE + REALM go to recipient at current market rate (uint256 realmOut, uint256 coreOut) = IUniswapV2Router(router) .removeLiquidityETH( address(realmToken), lp, 0, // accept market rate — LP holder accepts IL 0, _recipient, block.timestamp + 10 minutes ); // Release game rewards on top if (gameRew > 0) { require(realmToken.transfer(_recipient, gameRew), "Reward transfer failed"); } emit Withdrawal(nullifierHash, _recipient, coreOut, realmOut, gameRew); } // ─── GAME REWARD DISTRIBUTION ──────────────────────────── /** * @notice Receives REALM from Rewards_REALM contract on every game. * Called by Rewards_REALM.distributeFees() — must be authorised. * Distributes pro-rata to all active LP commitments via Masterchef. */ function receiveGameRewards(uint256 _amount) external nonReentrant { require(rewardSenders[msg.sender] || msg.sender == owner(), "Not authorised reward sender"); require(_amount > 0, "Zero amount"); require( realmToken.transferFrom(msg.sender, address(this), _amount), "Transfer failed" ); if (totalLpShares > 0) { accRewardPerShare += (_amount * 1e12) / totalLpShares; } // If no LPs yet, rewards held and distributed when first LP joins // (accRewardPerShare stays 0, new deposits enter at 0 rewardDebt) totalGameRewardsDistributed += _amount; emit GameRewardsReceived(_amount, accRewardPerShare); } // ─── REALM RESERVE FUNDING ─────────────────────────────── /** * @notice Fund the REALM reserve used to pair with LP deposits. * Dev calls this after deploying, using the 3.6M allocation. * Can also be called by DAO treasury or anyone who wants to contribute. * @param _amount REALM amount to add to reserve */ function fundRealm(uint256 _amount) external { require(_amount > 0, "Zero amount"); require( realmToken.transferFrom(msg.sender, address(this), _amount), "Transfer failed" ); realmReserve += _amount; emit RealmFunded(msg.sender, _amount); } // ─── VIEW HELPERS ──────────────────────────────────────── /** * @notice Check pending game rewards for a commitment. * Use this to check earnings without revealing nullifier. */ function pendingRewards(bytes32 _commitment) external view returns (uint256) { if (!commitments[_commitment]) return 0; uint256 lp = lpShares[_commitment]; uint256 accrued = (lp * accRewardPerShare) / 1e12; uint256 debt = rewardDebt[_commitment]; return accrued > debt ? accrued - debt + pendingExtra[_commitment] : pendingExtra[_commitment]; } /** * @notice Quote how much REALM will be paired with a given CORE deposit. */ function quoteDeposit(uint256 _coreAmount) external view returns ( uint256 realmNeeded, bool hasReserve ) { realmNeeded = _quoteRealmForCore(_coreAmount); hasReserve = realmReserve >= realmNeeded; } function getStats() external view returns ( uint256 _activeCommitments, uint256 _totalDeposited, uint256 _totalLpMinted, uint256 _realmReserve, uint256 _totalGameRewards ) { return ( activeCommitments, totalDeposited, totalLpMinted, realmReserve, totalGameRewardsDistributed ); } function _quoteRealmForCore(uint256 _coreAmount) internal view returns (uint256) { address wcore = IUniswapV2Router(router).WETH(); address[] memory path = new address[](2); path[0] = wcore; path[1] = address(realmToken); try IUniswapV2Router(router).getAmountsOut(_coreAmount, path) returns (uint256[] memory amounts) { return amounts[1]; } catch { // Pool doesn't exist yet — fallback placeholder return _coreAmount * 1000; // 1000 REALM per CORE fallback } } // ─── MERKLE TREE ───────────────────────────────────────── function _insertLeaf(bytes32 _leaf) internal { uint256 idx = nextIndex; bytes32 cur = _leaf; for (uint256 i = 0; i < MERKLE_TREE_HEIGHT; i++) { if (idx % 2 == 0) { filledSubtrees[i] = cur; cur = keccak256(abi.encodePacked(cur, filledSubtrees[i])); } else { cur = keccak256(abi.encodePacked(filledSubtrees[i], cur)); } idx /= 2; } root = cur; nextIndex++; } // ─── ADMIN ─────────────────────────────────────────────── function setRewardSender(address _sender, bool _status) external onlyOwner { rewardSenders[_sender] = _status; emit RewardSenderSet(_sender, _status); } function pause() external onlyOwner { _pause(); } function unpause() external onlyOwner { _unpause(); } /** * @notice Emergency: rescue non-CORE tokens (REALM only if paused). * CORE cannot be rescued — it belongs to LP providers. */ function rescueRealm(address _to, uint256 _amount) external onlyOwner { require(paused(), "Pause contract first"); realmToken.transfer(_to, _amount); } receive() external payable {} }. // SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT pragma solidity ^0.8.24; import "@openzeppelin/contracts-upgradeable/access/OwnableUpgradeable.sol"; } /** * @title Rewards_REALM v5 — UUPS Upgradeable Fee Distributor * * ─── WHAT CHANGED FROM v4 ──────────────────────────────────────────────────── * * [NEW] privateLpVault — address of PrivateLPVault_v2 * [NEW] privateLpBps — BPS slice of total fee routed to private LP vault * Default: 600 (6% of total fee) * Hard cap: MAX_PRIVATE_LP_BPS = 1500 (15%) * * [NEW] Step 5a in distributeFees(): * Before dev wallet receives remainder, privateLpBps% is carved out * and forwarded to vault.receiveGameRewards(amount). * If vault call fails (try/catch), amount stays with dev — no revert. * * [NEW] setPrivateLPVault(address) — owner sets vault address * [NEW] setPrivateLpBps(uint256) — owner sets LP cut (DAO-adjustable) * [NEW] totalPrivateLpFunded — lifetime stat tracker * [NEW] PrivateLpFunded event — on-chain audit trail * * [GAP] __gap reduced from [50] to [47] — 3 new storage slots consumed: * privateLpVault (address), privateLpBps (uint256), * totalPrivateLpFunded (uint256) * * ─── STORAGE LAYOUT RULES — READ BEFORE MODIFYING ─────────────────────────── * NEVER reorder, rename, or remove any existing variable. * New variables MUST be appended above __gap and __gap MUST shrink by same count. * Inherited slots come before these — do not list them here. * * ─── FEE SPLIT (of each player's 2.5% fee) ────────────────────────────────── * 10% → Cashback (both players) * 5% → Referral (if referrer set) * 8% → Creator bonus (private games only) * 14% → REALMStaking pool * 3% → PropertyNFT zone yield * 6% → PrivateLPVault (anonymous LP game rewards) ← NEW * ~54% → Dev wallet (remainder) * * ─── UPGRADE PATH ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── * 1. Dev wallet — remainder ───────────────────────────────────── if (remaining > 0) { require(realmToken.transfer(devWallet, remaining), "Dev transfer failed"); totalDevCollected += remaining; } totalFeesGenerated[_player1] += _feePerPlayer; totalFeesGenerated[_player2] += _feePerPlayer; emit FeesDistributed(totalFees, _player1, _player2, _gameType); } // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // CLAIM // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ function claimAll() external nonReentrant { uint256 total = cashbackBalance[msg.sender] + referralBalance[msg.sender] + creatorBalance[msg.sender]; require(total > 0, "Nothing to claim"); cashbackBalance[msg.sender] = 0; referralBalance[msg.sender] = 0; creatorBalance[msg.sender] = 0; require(realmToken.transfer(msg.sender, total), "Transfer failed"); emit RewardClaimed(msg.sender, total); } // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // SEASON PASS DISCOUNT // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ function effectiveFee(address _player, uint256 _baseFee) external view returns (uint256) { if (crossRealmNFT == address(0)) return _baseFee; uint256 discountBps = ICrossRealmNFT(crossRealmNFT).getSeasonPassDiscount(_player); if (discountBps == 0) return _baseFee; uint256 discount = (_baseFee * discountBps) / BASIS_POINTS; return _baseFee > discount ?
